SELECT r1."Id", r1."Username", r1."Email", r0."Name" AS "Role", r1."RoleId", r1."Designation", d."Name" AS "Department", r1."DepartmentId", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Rejected'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"

END AS "totalQuantity", i."Description" AS description
FROM "Items" AS i
INNER JOIN "Categories" AS c ON i."CategoryId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "InventoryStocks" AS i0 ON i."Id" = i0."ItemId"

    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'

END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"

2026-05-25 19:25:03.034 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (13ms) [Parameters=[@p1='?' (DbType = Int32), @p='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT r0."Id", r0."UserId", u."Username", u."Email", CASE r0."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Requested'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'Issued'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
    ELSE r0."Status"::text
END, r0."CreatedAt", r0."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r0."UserId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r1."Id" AS id, r1."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r1."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", i."Id" AS "Id0", r1."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r1
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r1."ItemId" = i."Id"
) AS s ON r0."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r0."CreatedAt" DESC, r0."Id", u."Id", s.id

    WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'Issued'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
    ELSE r0."Status"::text
END, r0."CreatedAt", r0."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r0."UserId" = u."Id"

    SELECT r1."Id" AS id, r1."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r1."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", i."Id" AS "Id0", r1."RequestId"

) AS s ON r0."Id" = s."RequestId"

SELECT r0."Id", r0."UserId", u."Username", u."Email", CASE r0."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Requested'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'Issued'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
    ELSE r0."Status"::text
END, r0."CreatedAt", r0."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r0."UserId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r1."Id" AS id, r1."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r1."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", i."Id" AS "Id0", r1."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r1
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r1."ItemId" = i."Id"
) AS s ON r0."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r0."CreatedAt" DESC, r0."Id", u."Id", s.id

END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"

SELECT r1."Id", r1."Username", r1."Email", r0."Name" AS "Role", r1."RoleId", r1."Designation", d."Name" AS "Department", r1."DepartmentId", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Rejected'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."DepartmentId", r."Designation", r."Email", r."RoleId", r."Status", r."Username"
    FROM "RegistrationRequests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC, r."Id" DESC
    LIMIT @p
) AS r1
INNER JOIN "Roles" AS r0 ON r1."RoleId" = r0."Id"
INNER JOIN "Departments" AS d ON r1."DepartmentId" = d."Id"
ORDER BY r1."CreatedAt" DESC, r1."Id" DESC

2026-05-25 21:39:20.544 +00:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (4ms) [Parameters=[@p1='?' (DbType = Int32), @p='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT r0."Id", r0."UserId", u."Username", u."Email", CASE r0."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Requested'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Rejected'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'Issued'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Received'
    ELSE r0."Status"::text
END, r0."CreatedAt", r0."UpdatedAt", u."Id", s.id, s."itemId", s."itemName", s."quantityRequested", s."quantityIssued", s."Id0"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."Status", r."UpdatedAt", r."UserId"
    FROM "Requests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 4
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON r0."UserId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r1."Id" AS id, r1."ItemId" AS "itemId", i."Name" AS "itemName", r1."QuantityRequested" AS "quantityRequested", r1."QuantityIssued" AS "quantityIssued", i."Id" AS "Id0", r1."RequestId"
    FROM "RequestItems" AS r1
    INNER JOIN "Items" AS i ON r1."ItemId" = i."Id"
) AS s ON r0."Id" = s."RequestId"
ORDER BY r0."CreatedAt" DESC, r0."Id", u."Id", s.id
